		  |bcu.turn_off_alarm -> Q2222
		  |ms[1].detected -> Q2338
		  |bcu.req_on[1] -> Q2558
		  |sprinkler[1].on -> Q2585
		  |sensor[1].detected -> Q3549
		  |alarm[1].on -> Q4027)
